3723 WCHAR ff_convert ( /* Converted code, 0 means conversion error */
3724  WCHAR chr, /* Character code to be converted */
3725  UINT dir /* 0: Unicode to OEM code, 1: OEM code to Unicode */
3726 )
3727 {
3728  const WCHAR *p;
3729  WCHAR c;
3730  int i, n, li, hi;
3731 
3732 
3733  if (chr <= 0x80) { /* ASCII */
3734  c = chr;
3735  } else {
3736 #if !_TINY_TABLE
3737  if (dir) { /* OEM code to unicode */
3738  p = sjis2uni;
3739  hi = sizeof sjis2uni / 4 - 1;
3740  } else { /* Unicode to OEM code */
3741  p = uni2sjis;
3742  hi = sizeof uni2sjis / 4 - 1;
3743  }
3744  li = 0;
3745  for (n = 16; n; n--) {
3746  i = li + (hi - li) / 2;
3747  if (chr == p[i * 2]) break;
3748  if (chr > p[i * 2])
3749  li = i;
3750  else
3751  hi = i;
3752  }
3753  c = n ? p[i * 2 + 1] : 0;
3754 #else
3755  if (dir) { /* OEM code to unicode (Incremental search)*/
3756  p = &uni2sjis[1];
3757  do {
3758  c = *p;
3759  p += 2;
3760  } while (c && c != chr);
3761  p -= 3;
3762  c = *p;
3763  } else { /* Unicode to OEM code */
3764  li = 0; hi = sizeof uni2sjis / 4 - 1;
3765  for (n = 16; n; n--) {
3766  i = li + (hi - li) / 2;
3767  if (chr == uni2sjis[i * 2]) break;
3768  if (chr > uni2sjis[i * 2])
3769  li = i;
3770  else
3771  hi = i;
3772  }
3773  c = n ? uni2sjis[i * 2 + 1] : 0;
3774  }
3775 #endif
3776  }
3777 
3778  return c;
3779 }
3780

3783 WCHAR ff_wtoupper ( /* Returns upper converted character */
3784  WCHAR chr /* Unicode character to be upper converted (BMP only) */
3785 )
3786 {
3787  /* Compressed upper conversion table */
3788  static const WCHAR cvt1[] = { /* U+0000 - U+0FFF */
3789  /* Basic Latin */
3790  0x0061,0x031A,
3791  /* Latin-1 Supplement */
3792  0x00E0,0x0317, 0x00F8,0x0307, 0x00FF,0x0001,0x0178,
3793  /* Latin Extended-A */
3794  0x0100,0x0130, 0x0132,0x0106, 0x0139,0x0110, 0x014A,0x012E, 0x0179,0x0106,
3795  /* Latin Extended-B */
3796  0x0180,0x004D,0x0243,0x0181,0x0182,0x0182,0x0184,0x0184,0x0186,0x0187,0x0187,0x0189,0x018A,0x018B,0x018B,0x018D,0x018E,0x018F,0x0190,0x0191,0x0191,0x0193,0x0194,0x01F6,0x0196,0x0197,0x0198,0x0198,0x023D,0x019B,0x019C,0x019D,0x0220,0x019F,0x01A0,0x01A0,0x01A2,0x01A2,0x01A4,0x01A4,0x01A6,0x01A7,0x01A7,0x01A9,0x01AA,0x01AB,0x01AC,0x01AC,0x01AE,0x01AF,0x01AF,0x01B1,0x01B2,0x01B3,0x01B3,0x01B5,0x01B5,0x01B7,0x01B8,0x01B8,0x01BA,0x01BB,0x01BC,0x01BC,0x01BE,0x01F7,0x01C0,0x01C1,0x01C2,0x01C3,0x01C4,0x01C5,0x01C4,0x01C7,0x01C8,0x01C7,0x01CA,0x01CB,0x01CA,
3797  0x01CD,0x0110, 0x01DD,0x0001,0x018E, 0x01DE,0x0112, 0x01F3,0x0003,0x01F1,0x01F4,0x01F4, 0x01F8,0x0128,
3798  0x0222,0x0112, 0x023A,0x0009,0x2C65,0x023B,0x023B,0x023D,0x2C66,0x023F,0x0240,0x0241,0x0241, 0x0246,0x010A,
3799  /* IPA Extensions */
3800  0x0253,0x0040,0x0181,0x0186,0x0255,0x0189,0x018A,0x0258,0x018F,0x025A,0x0190,0x025C,0x025D,0x025E,0x025F,0x0193,0x0261,0x0262,0x0194,0x0264,0x0265,0x0266,0x0267,0x0197,0x0196,0x026A,0x2C62,0x026C,0x026D,0x026E,0x019C,0x0270,0x0271,0x019D,0x0273,0x0274,0x019F,0x0276,0x0277,0x0278,0x0279,0x027A,0x027B,0x027C,0x2C64,0x027E,0x027F,0x01A6,0x0281,0x0282,0x01A9,0x0284,0x0285,0x0286,0x0287,0x01AE,0x0244,0x01B1,0x01B2,0x0245,0x028D,0x028E,0x028F,0x0290,0x0291,0x01B7,
3801  /* Greek, Coptic */
3802  0x037B,0x0003,0x03FD,0x03FE,0x03FF, 0x03AC,0x0004,0x0386,0x0388,0x0389,0x038A, 0x03B1,0x0311,
3803  0x03C2,0x0002,0x03A3,0x03A3, 0x03C4,0x0308, 0x03CC,0x0003,0x038C,0x038E,0x038F, 0x03D8,0x0118,
3804  0x03F2,0x000A,0x03F9,0x03F3,0x03F4,0x03F5,0x03F6,0x03F7,0x03F7,0x03F9,0x03FA,0x03FA,
3805  /* Cyrillic */
3806  0x0430,0x0320, 0x0450,0x0710, 0x0460,0x0122, 0x048A,0x0136, 0x04C1,0x010E, 0x04CF,0x0001,0x04C0, 0x04D0,0x0144,
3807  /* Armenian */
3808  0x0561,0x0426,
3809 
3810  0x0000
3811  };
3812  static const WCHAR cvt2[] = { /* U+1000 - U+FFFF */
3813  /* Phonetic Extensions */
3814  0x1D7D,0x0001,0x2C63,
3815  /* Latin Extended Additional */
3816  0x1E00,0x0196, 0x1EA0,0x015A,
3817  /* Greek Extended */
3818  0x1F00,0x0608, 0x1F10,0x0606, 0x1F20,0x0608, 0x1F30,0x0608, 0x1F40,0x0606,
3819  0x1F51,0x0007,0x1F59,0x1F52,0x1F5B,0x1F54,0x1F5D,0x1F56,0x1F5F, 0x1F60,0x0608,
3820  0x1F70,0x000E,0x1FBA,0x1FBB,0x1FC8,0x1FC9,0x1FCA,0x1FCB,0x1FDA,0x1FDB,0x1FF8,0x1FF9,0x1FEA,0x1FEB,0x1FFA,0x1FFB,
3821  0x1F80,0x0608, 0x1F90,0x0608, 0x1FA0,0x0608, 0x1FB0,0x0004,0x1FB8,0x1FB9,0x1FB2,0x1FBC,
3822  0x1FCC,0x0001,0x1FC3, 0x1FD0,0x0602, 0x1FE0,0x0602, 0x1FE5,0x0001,0x1FEC, 0x1FF2,0x0001,0x1FFC,
3823  /* Letterlike Symbols */
3824  0x214E,0x0001,0x2132,
3825  /* Number forms */
3826  0x2170,0x0210, 0x2184,0x0001,0x2183,
3827  /* Enclosed Alphanumerics */
3828  0x24D0,0x051A, 0x2C30,0x042F,
3829  /* Latin Extended-C */
3830  0x2C60,0x0102, 0x2C67,0x0106, 0x2C75,0x0102,
3831  /* Coptic */
3832  0x2C80,0x0164,
3833  /* Georgian Supplement */
3834  0x2D00,0x0826,
3835  /* Full-width */
3836  0xFF41,0x031A,
3837 
3838  0x0000
3839  };
3840  const WCHAR *p;
3841  WCHAR bc, nc, cmd;
3842 
3843 
3844  p = chr < 0x1000 ? cvt1 : cvt2;
3845  for (;;) {
3846  bc = *p++; /* Get block base */
3847  if (!bc || chr < bc) break;
3848  nc = *p++; cmd = nc >> 8; nc &= 0xFF; /* Get processing command and block size */
3849  if (chr < bc + nc) { /* In the block? */
3850  switch (cmd) {
3851  case 0: chr = p[chr - bc]; break; /* Table conversion */
3852  case 1: chr -= (chr - bc) & 1; break; /* Case pairs */
3853  case 2: chr -= 16; break; /* Shift -16 */
3854  case 3: chr -= 32; break; /* Shift -32 */
3855  case 4: chr -= 48; break; /* Shift -48 */
3856  case 5: chr -= 26; break; /* Shift -26 */
3857  case 6: chr += 8; break; /* Shift +8 */
3858  case 7: chr -= 80; break; /* Shift -80 */
3859  case 8: chr -= 0x1C60; break; /* Shift -0x1C60 */
3860  }
3861  break;
3862  }
3863  if (!cmd) p += nc;
3864  }
3865 
3866  return chr;
3867 }
